## Use Cases
### UC-1: Serve intraday bars with executable fallback
- Actors: dashboard chart consumer, `/api/zl/intraday` route
- Preconditions: 15-minute table can be sparse while 1-minute table contains bars
- Flow:
  - Query `mkt.price_15m`
  - If unusable/empty, query `mkt.price_1m`
  - Return normalized envelope with accurate `source`
- Postconditions: route behavior matches declared fallback contract
- Requirement links: `REQ-001`

### UC-2A: Target-zones route canonical envelope
- Actors: dashboard bootstrap loader
- Preconditions: latest `forecasts.target_zones` rows exist
- Flow:
  - Fetch `/api/zl/target-zones`
  - Parse canonical envelope contract
- Postconditions: payload is compatible with shared client contract
- Requirement links: `REQ-002`

### UC-2B: Forecast-targets route canonical envelope
- Actors: probability surface loader
- Preconditions: latest `forecasts.target_zones` rows exist
- Flow:
  - Fetch `/api/zl/forecast-targets`
  - Parse same envelope contract as sibling route (or adapter-backed equivalent)
- Postconditions: route-level parser divergence is eliminated
- Requirement links: `REQ-002`

### UC-3: Record ingest run lifecycle with one vocabulary
- Actors: SQL ingest jobs, TS ingest helper, ops analytics readers
- Preconditions: ingest run starts and reaches terminal state
- Flow:
  - Write start lifecycle row
  - Update terminal status with canonical vocabulary
- Postconditions: status analytics are deterministic across producers
- Requirement links: `REQ-003`

### UC-4: Approval-gated training and promotion execution
- Actors: pipeline operator, train/promote phases
- Preconditions: non-dry execution requested
- Flow:
  - Dispatch phase through pipeline
  - Enforce explicit approval requirement
- Postconditions: unauthorized train/promote execution is blocked
- Requirement links: `REQ-004`

### UC-5: Degraded-mode transparency during runtime pull outages
- Actors: AI-first card route consumers
- Preconditions: runtime trusted-market pull fails or degrades
- Flow:
  - Route attempts pull
  - Route emits fallback output with provenance metadata
- Postconditions: consumers can distinguish degraded from fully fresh responses
- Requirement links: `REQ-005`

### UC-6: Operator startup documentation consistency
- Actors: maintainers and new operators
- Preconditions: onboarding/startup instructions are consulted
- Flow:
  - Read root/operator docs
  - Validate no conflict with authority startup constraints
- Postconditions: startup behavior does not rely on prohibited hardcoded-port assumptions
- Requirement links: `REQ-006`

### UC-7: Generate per-bug writeups at canonical path
- Actors: code review/spec audit phase outputs
- Preconditions: bug is confirmed
- Flow:
  - Create writeup file under `quality/writeups/`
- Postconditions: bug handoff artifact exists at canonical location
- Requirement links: `REQ-007`

### UC-8: Generate fix patch at canonical path
- Actors: reconciliation phase patch generation
- Preconditions: bug has proposed code fix
- Flow:
  - Emit `BUG-<id>-fix.patch` under `quality/patches/`
- Postconditions: fix patch path contract satisfied
- Requirement links: `REQ-008`

# Requirements: ZINC-FUSION-V16
> Generated by [Quality Playbook](https://github.com/andrewstellman/quality-playbook) v1.5.3 — Andrew Stellman
> Date: 2026-05-16 · Project: ZINC-FUSION-V16

## Project Overview
These requirements are derived from `quality/EXPLORATION.md` Phase 1 findings and govern forecast route contracts, ingestion telemetry consistency, approval-gated model operations, runtime data-source resilience, and the canonical quality-artifact layout for this run.

## Requirements
### REQ-001: Intraday fallback execution parity
- Statement: `app/api/zl/intraday` must execute the declared 15m->1m fallback behavior when primary query returns no usable bars.
- Tier: 3
- Source type: code-derived
- Pattern: parity
- References:
  - `app/api/zl/intraday/route.ts:16-23`
  - `supabase/migrations/202603180002_mkt.sql:18-19`
- Linked use cases: `UC-1`
- Conditions of satisfaction:
  - `GET()` includes an executable branch that queries `mkt.price_1m` when `mkt.price_15m` produces no usable rows.
  - Response `source` reflects the table actually used for the payload.
  - Fallback behavior is mechanically testable by source-level contract assertions in `quality/test_functional.py`.

### REQ-002: Forecast-target envelope parity
- Statement: Forecast target endpoints must expose one stable envelope contract for equivalent semantic payloads.
- Tier: 3
- Source type: code-derived
- Pattern: parity
- References:
  - `app/api/zl/target-zones/route.ts:80-87`
  - `app/api/zl/forecast-targets/route.ts:103-106`
  - `components/dashboard/ProbabilitySurface.tsx:62-83`
- Linked use cases: `UC-2A`, `UC-2B`
- Conditions of satisfaction:
  - `/api/zl/target-zones` and `/api/zl/forecast-targets` either emit the same envelope keys or publish explicit typed adapters consumed by all clients.
  - Success and error payload contracts are parsable by one canonical client-side adapter path.
  - Horizon normalization behavior remains equivalent across both routes.

### REQ-003: Canonical `ops.ingest_run.status` vocabulary
- Statement: All writers to `ops.ingest_run.status` must share one canonical status vocabulary.
- Tier: 3
